## ‚ö° EARLIER ‚Äî 2026-06-23 **E1 / S3 ALT-HISTORY: "YOUR WAR vs HISTORY" ‚Äî a living divergence ledger of every point your war has left the documented record, with the history each entry departs from + an emergent-only toggle** (overnight run, D111)

> **The Phase-E strategic arc opens.** The GM ¬ß12 depth-chart arc is COMPLETE (Appoint/Relieve ¬∑ Promote ¬∑ Corps ¬∑ Commission ¬∑ Division). Each entry carries a **category** (Emancipation / Foreign / Northern politics / The war's trajectory / Wild cards), a **tier** (minor ‚ñ≥ / major ‚óÜ / radical ‚òÖ ‚Äî distance from the record, CVD-safe glyph+word+colour), a short **when**, and the **historical counterfactual** ("In history, ‚Ä¶") that is the lesson. A headline **DIVERGENCE INDEX** (0..100, a saturating tier-weight sum + a 5-step word ladder) measures how far the war has strayed. ## ‚ö° EARLIER ‚Äî 2026-06-23 **Q12: THE DIVISION SUB-TIER ‚Äî seat your generals into the DIVISION billets nested under each corps; a corps is only as good as its divisions** (overnight run, D110 ‚Äî Codex code + Claude vetting/doc close-out)

> **The GM depth-chart's next rung is shipped** (RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN ¬ß12.1 ‚Äî Army ‚Üí Corps ‚Üí **DIVISION** ‚Üí Brigade), built on the Q10 corps chart (D108). Beyond seating I‚ÄìIV Corps, the President now SEATS pool generals into each seated corps's **3 DIVISION billets**, spending **political capital** (`C.clock.capital`, the existing GM currency). A division can be staffed ONLY under a SEATED corps (the real chain of command), so the depth chart is a TREE built top-down. Teaches that a corps was only as good as its divisions ‚Äî A. P. Hill's "Light Division" and Hood's/Pickett's divisions were the cutting edge of Lee's corps, **as were the Union's hard-fighting divisions in Hancock's II Corps**.

Gen.'s** billet in BOTH armies (distinct from the corps tier where a CS corps was a Lt. Gen.'s), so any Brig. Gen. seated over a division leads stretched until promoted. The lift is deliberately SMALLER than the corps lift (cap 2 vs 4) so the hierarchy holds: **army ¬±17 > corps ¬±4 > divisions ¬±2.** No division seated ‚Üí Œ£ over zero slots ‚Üí lift 0 ‚Üí the sandbox + all 9 battles identical to HEAD `7d86fcf`. **ONE BILLET PER MAN** (army/corps/division mutually exclusive; seating-higher clears the division); **vacating a corps CASCADES** (orphaned divisions stop contributing lift ‚Äî enforced at the READ layer `cmdDivSeated`/`_cmdDivLift`, cleaned on load-sanitize). `cmd.divisions = {corpsIdx:{divIdx:id}}` rides the save (no `_SAVE_VER` bump); `cmdInit` sanitizes a tampered record on load. Writes ONLY `cmd.divisions` + capital (build-gate 4d scans `35-command.js`). NO RNG. `data/ratings.json` `divisionCommand` (Inferred + 2 sources: Glatthaar, Weigley).

## ‚ö° EARLIER ‚Äî 2026-06-23 **Q10: THE CORPS DEPTH-CHART ‚Äî seat your generals into corps command over the Order-of-Battle tree; who you place (and whether his rank fits the billet) shapes how well the whole army fights** (overnight run, D108)

> **The GM depth-chart MOVE is shipped, built on the D106 OOB tree** (RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN ¬ß12.1/¬ß12.2/¬ß12.4 ‚Äî "an army version of waiver/trading/transfer"). Beyond appointing the ARMY commander (the existing `cmdAppoint` billet), a new President's-Desk **"The Corps Command ‚Äî Depth Chart"** section lets the President SEAT pool generals into the army's CORPS billets (I‚ÄìIV Corps), spending **political capital** (`C.clock.capital` ‚Äî the existing GM currency, no new resource). Each billet shows its seated commander (name + grade + OVR + a below-grade tell) with a Vacate control, or "Vacant" + a pool `<select>` + a Seat control (gated on capital); a live read-out shows the net leadership the staffed corps add. Teaches real command organization ‚Äî Lee's First (Longstreet) and Second (Jackson) Corps vs the Army of the Potomac's churning corps commands; the rout of Howard's XI Corps at Chancellorsville.
>
> **PICK RATIONALE (decide-&-log within the cleared NEXT menu):** chose the depth-chart MOVES (option A) over the symmetric AI-GM (option B, flagged [hard]) because A extends the proven `cmdAppoint`/`cmdPromote` spine over the D106 substrate and is byte-identical-until-moved like Q9; the new officer-slot/vacancy concept the derived T15 corps lacked is the `cmd.corps` slot map + a side-aware grade-fit.
>
> **HOW IT REACHES THE FIGHT (no new combat path; D74/D94 no-fudge):** seated corps commanders only add a small BOUNDED lift to `commandLeadership(C)` ‚Äî an INPUT the bridge already reads ‚Äî via `_cmdCorpsLift(C)` = `clamp( SUM over seated slots of (effectiveCorpsRating ‚àí 64) √ó perSlotWeight, ¬±liftCap )` (0.05 / cap 4). `effectiveCorpsRating` = the general's GM OVR (carries the Q9 promotion lift) minus `belowGradePenalty` (6) when his CURRENT grade is below the **SIDE-AWARE** preferred grade. It reaches combat ONLY through the existing `commandLeadership ‚Üí bridge LEADERSHIP facet` pipe, NEVER the scoreboard (build-gate 4d scans `35-command.js` + `tactical/T15-oob.js`). The army commander still weighs most (~¬±17); the corps lift (¬±4) is a secondary modifier (¬ß27).
>
> **THE SIDE-AWARE GRADE-FIT (historically precise; the Q9 synergy):** a US corps was a **Maj. Gen.'s** command, a CS corps a **Lt. Gen.'s** (the CS authorized the Lt. Gen. grade Sept. 18, 1862, promoting Longstreet/Jackson that Oct. to command the ANV's new corps). So on the shipped roster only CS **Stuart** (a Maj. Gen.) seats below grade over a corps; promoting him to Lt. Gen. (Q9) removes the penalty. `data/ratings.json` `corpsCommand`: `slots 4 ¬∑ seatCost 3 ¬∑ preferredGrade {US:"Maj. Gen.",CS:"Lt. Gen."} ¬∑ perSlotWeight 0.05 ¬∑ liftCap 4 ¬∑ belowGradePenalty 6 ¬∑ Inferred ¬∑ 2 sources`.
>
> **BYTE-IDENTICAL until you seat a corps:** no corps seated ‚Üí lift 0 ‚Üí `commandLeadership` unchanged ‚Üí the sandbox + all 9 battles identical to HEAD `2d11bd7` (a vacant billet contributes 0, NOT a penalty). `cmd.corps` rides the save (no `_SAVE_VER` bump); `cmdInit` sanitizes a tampered/imported record on LOAD (drop invalid slots/ids/dead generals/the army commander; one corps per general; array‚Üí{}). The army commander can't double-hold (excluded from the pool; `cmdAppoint` clears his corps). The seated commanders also NAME the player's DERIVED corps on the OOB board (pure display ‚Äî the predicted edge is UNCHANGED; the enemy is never named; a "Garrison" node is never named).
>
> **Bug-hunt: 11 Opus agents (5 diverse lenses √ó default-refute verify + a completeness critic) ‚Üí invariantsHold = TRUE** (the critic independently grep-confirmed no combat path reads `cmd.corps`, seat/vacate write only `cmd.corps`+capital, byte-identity airtight, no fabricated officers, the 2 sources real). **3 confirmed (1 MED + 2 LOW), ALL FIXED:** **(MED)** the seat-log said "leads **above** his grade" for a BELOW-grade general ‚Üí "below". **(LOW)** a real general could be named over a derived **"Garrison"** node (a fort/detachment, not a corps) ‚Üí the attach now guards to `/ Corps$/` nodes only (probe-locked). **(LOW)** the CS Lt. ## ‚ö° EARLIER ‚Äî 2026-06-22 **RATING SYSTEM Q9 ‚Äî the GM PROMOTION economy (the first depth-chart MOVE: promote ¬∑ multi-currency ¬∑ merit gate)** (overnight run, D102)

> **The first real GM *move* beyond appoint/relieve is shipped.** On the President's-Desk Command tab there is now an **"Officer Corps ‚Äî Promotions"** section: the President promotes a general one grade up a clean strategic ladder (**Brig. Gen. ‚Üí Maj. Gen. ‚Üí Lt. Gen. ‚Üí General**), spending a **multi-currency** budget ‚Äî **political capital** (`C.clock.capital`, the primary, shared with relief/appointment) **+ a NEW seniority pool** (`cmd.seniority`, accrues over the campaign, capped) ‚Äî and **merit-gated** by reputation. PURE INPUT-SEEDING + display, **byte-identical until the player promotes** (sandbox + all 9 battles proven byte-for-byte identical to committed HEAD `fc1d251`). Built on the existing `cmdAppoint`/`_cmdReliefCost` spine + the R-5 `fldPromotePerson` latent-command concept; entirely in `src/35-command.js` (the "Q9 (D102)" block) + a `promotion` config in `data/ratings.json`.
>
> **THE MERIT GATE (the honest history, the keystone):** each target grade carries a reputation **meritBar**. EARNED (rep ‚â• bar) ‚Üí a confidence bump (+3 rep); ABOVE merit (rep < bar) ‚Üí a √ó1.8 capital surcharge **+ a jealousy reputation HIT (‚àí4)**. Because OVR = 0.55¬∑skill + 0.45¬∑reputation, **over-promoting a favorite past his record can LOWER his OVR** ‚Äî rank without merit doesn't make a good commander (teaches the real command politics Lincoln navigated; anti-Lost-Cause: merit, not grade, is competence). Leapfrogging a passed-over senior adds a seniority surcharge.
>
> **HOW IT REACHES THE FIGHT (no new combat path, no fudge):** a promotion lifts the general's effective skill by a small **BOUNDED** amount ‚Äî `_cmdPromoteSkillLift` = (rankBase grade-delta √ó 0.92), clamped to **‚â§6** ‚Äî added inside the EDITED `_cmdEffectiveSkill(gen, C)`, which flows ONLY through the existing `_cmdGenRating ‚Üí commandLeadership ‚Üí` the bridge LEADERSHIP facet (an INPUT the sim already reads; `commandMarginEdge` reads aggression/caution, untouched). `cmdPromote` writes ONLY `clk.capital`/`cmd.seniority`/`cmd.promotions`/`cmd.reputation` ‚Äî **never the scoreboard** (D74/D94 wall). **0 lift when un-promoted ‚Üí every pre-Q9 reading byte-identical** (live-sanity proven: a promotion stores "Lt. Gen.", lifts commandLeadership 79‚Üí80; the un-promoted skill reads identical with/without C for all 20 generals).
>
> **New fns (`src/35-command.js`):** `_cmdPromoCfg`/`_cmdRankBase`/`_cmdBaseGrade`/`_cmdGradeIdx`/`_cmdNextGrade`/`_cmdCurrentGrade`/`_cmdPromoteSkillLift`/`_cmdLeapfrogged`/`_cmdPromoteInfo`/`cmdPromote`/`_cmdPromoRow`/`_cmdPromotionsHTML`/`_cmdNum`; EDITED `_cmdEffectiveSkill(gen,C)` (+lift), `cmdInit` (seeds + load-clamps `seniority`, seeds `promotions`), `cmdOnResolve` (accrues `seniority` ‚Äî invisible/byte-identical), `cmdRenderTab` (+section), `cmdWireTab` (+promote buttons); call sites `_cmdGenRating`/`cmdActiveTraits`/`_cmdActiveCard` now thread C. **Data:** the `promotion` block in `data/ratings.json` (ladder ¬∑ meritBar ¬∑ capitalCost ¬∑ aboveMeritMul ¬∑ seniority{CostBase,Leapfrog,Start,PerTurn,WinBonus,Cap} ¬∑ earnedRepBonus ¬∑ aboveMeritRepHit ¬∑ skillLiftWeight ¬∑ skillLiftCap ¬∑ topCommandPreferredGrade).
>
> **Bug-hunt (7 Opus agents: 4 diverse-lens finders √ó default-refute verify + a completeness critic; 2 raw ‚Üí 2 confirmed + 1 actionable critic gap, ALL LOW + LATENT; 0 HIGH/MED; critic: "SOUND, may commit ‚Äî no-fudge/byte-identity/bounding/determinism/no-exploit all hold; no HIGH/MED missed").** ALL 3 fixed: (1) `cmdPromote` gated on `round(capital)` but spent raw ‚Üí now debits the rounded `cap` (one lens; byte-identical under integer paths); (2) `_cmdBaseGrade`'s unrecognized-rank fallback "Maj. (lowest; hardens the deferred depth-chart path); (3) `cmdInit` now re-clamps a tampered/stale out-of-band `seniority` to the cap on LOAD. ## ‚ö° EARLIER ‚Äî 2026-06-22 **RATING SYSTEM R-5 ‚Äî the PROSOPOGRAPHY SCALE-OUT (bulk per-person rows + lazy materialization + play-as-anyone)** (overnight run, D101)

> **The D93 "Soldier's Story" substrate the whole rating spine was built for is shipped.** A brigade can now be inspected down to its men, any person *materialized* + *promoted*, and a generated soldier carries a deterministic name + Inferred rating ‚Äî all **PURE DATA + DISPLAY**, **byte-identical** (no shipped scenario assigns bulk persons; sandbox + all 9 battles proven IDENTICAL to committed HEAD `84c5e95`). Selecting a brigade now shows its **MEN OVR** (the men's prosopography mean) beside the R-2 combat OVR, with a provenance-hatched accent.
>
> **THE LAZY-MATERIALIZATION KEYSTONE (¬ß8) ‚Äî the whole point of R-5:** a brigade TOKEN carries ONE aggregate `fldMenMeanOVR(u,year)` (its men's mean OVR, derived **O(1)** from xp + arm-branch + year + a deterministic per-brigade-id jitter, clamped [20,88] ‚Äî a brigade AVERAGE never reaches the Legendary individual ceiling). Per-person rows are **NEVER instantiated en masse:** `fldMaterializePerson(spec,year)` builds exactly ONE row on demand; `fldBrigadeMuster(u,n,year)` a **HARD-CAPPED (‚â§6)** representative sample (captain/sergeant/private from `data/ratings.json` `musterTemplate`) ‚Äî **never `u.men` rows** (proven: a 100,000-man brigade still materializes 3). The mean is always recomputable, never the source of truth (so a future zoom-to-regiment is a roll-up of materialized rows).
>
> **New pure functions (`src/tactical/T14-ratings.js`, the R-5 section):** `fldMenMeanOVR` ¬∑ `fldMaterializePerson` (reuses R-0 `fldDerivePerson` ‚Üí headline + dual OVR + grade; generated ‚Üí deterministic synth period name [`_fldSynthName`/`_FLD_FIRST`/`_FLD_LAST`, NO RNG] + Inferred + a `latentCommand` seed; authored ‚Üí Verified pass-through) ¬∑ **`fldPromotePerson(person,toRank)`** (the latent-command **play-as-anyone** promotion ‚Äî lifts command/tactical/discipline/charisma by the rank-base delta; returns a NEW person, pure) ¬∑ `fldPersonTeam` (the EA-style {side,army,corps} journey hook) ¬∑ `fldProvenanceStyle` (the **Inferred-vs-Verified visual distinction** ¬ß10 ‚Äî Verified SOLID / Inferred **HATCHED** `repeating-linear-gradient` / Disputed dashed; meaning rides pattern + glyph [‚úì/~/?] + word, NOT colour ‚Üí CVD-safe) ¬∑ `fldMusterHudLine` (the live compact line) ¬∑ **`fldMusterRollHtml`** (the full "Muster Roll" panel ‚Äî probe-vetted + ready for the journey-mode character sheet / Army Register). **Live wiring = ONE guarded line** in `fldRenderHud` (`src/tactical/T0-field-sandbox.js`). NO new combat path; NO RNG.

## ‚ö° CONTINUE HERE ‚Äî 2026-06-22 **RATING SYSTEM R-4 ‚Äî the X-FACTORS (the dramatic "in the zone" surge, inside the no-fudge wall)** (overnight run, D98)

> **The Madden layer now SWINGS a fight ‚Äî provably without ever touching the scoreboard.** An X-Factor badge enters "in the zone" when its situational trigger fires and surges on ONE channel, hard-capped. Demonstrated: a single `foot_cavalry` badge on one CS sandbox brigade **flipped a deterministic US win into a CS win** (same seed), yet the total-casualty shift was only **17.2%** and the command aura peaked at **0.47 < the 0.9 wall** ‚Äî the rating reaches the result EMERGENTLY through bounded inputs, never by writing `cas`/`victory`/`men`/`sev`.
>
> **`fldXFactorStep(dt)` (`src/tactical/T14-ratings.js`):** gated on `__FIELD.badges`; for each unit carrying an `rung:"xfactor"` badge (`_fldUnitXFactors`), `_fldXFactorInZone` tests activation (march_vigor=moving ¬∑ his_offensive=moving/charging ¬∑ ammo_low_defend=ammo<12 & not charging ¬∑ last_stand_defend=holding & (low morale or a friendly routing within 220yd) ¬∑ usct_assault/mass_assault=charging ¬∑ flanking=cav & charging). In the zone it surges **ONE channel = the declared lever**: a NON-speed X-Factor sets `u._xfActive = fldRatingRealismCap(tier,"xfactor")` (arcade 1.45 / balanced 1.20 / historian 1.08); a SPEED X-Factor (Foot Cavalry / The Slows) sets `u._spdMul` only (capped [0.85,1.15]) and does NOT also surge the aura. One-shot ‚ö° `fldAnnounce`+`fldScenarioBanner` (`_xfOn` rising edge); `_xfGlow` marker pulse; deterministic `_fldXfDecay`‚Üí1 out of zone. **NO RNG.** A unit with no X-Factor is wholly untouched ‚Üí byte-identical.
>
> **`fldXFactorApplyCmd(u)`:** `u.cmdBonus = min(FLDO.CMD_BONUS_CAP, (cmdBonus||0)*_xfActive)` ‚Äî pushes the summed aura toward the **0.9 wall, never beyond**; strict no-op unless active. Called in `fldSimStep` AFTER `fldOfficersStep` (aura summed first), gated on `badges` (NOT officers) so both surge channels share one gate.
>
> **Seams (`src/tactical/T0-field-sandbox.js`):** `fldSimStep` runs the surge + apply around `fldOfficersStep`; **`fldMoveFactor` clamps the COMBINED speed factor** (the `_spdMul` surge √ó the R-3 static speed-badge factor) to ONE documented band **[0.75,1.30]** (exactly 1 ‚Üí skipped ‚Üí byte-identical); `fld2dDraw` draws a guarded `_xfGlow` ‚Äî a CVD-safe amber burst RING (the shape carries meaning) + a **vector-drawn** lightning bolt (no emoji-font tofu), `reduceMotion`-honored. **Data:** added `first_with_the_most` (Forrest, cav) ‚Üí 7 X-Factors; none assigned to a shipped roster yet (R-6) ‚Üí byte-identical.
>
> **Vet:** GATE OK (no-fudge ‚úì); `probe-ratings` **17/17** (the R-4 surge step + the NO-FUDGE REPLAY GATE: the surge bites + bounded + capped); the **`domcontentloaded` byte-identity harness IDENTICAL for all 10** (sandbox + 9 battles, R-4 build vs committed R-3 HEAD ‚Äî the authoritative X-Factor-off no-regression proof); `tactical-visuals` 10/10 scenes 0 pe; `diag-classic` `nonBlank:346`; the 9 battle probes + field + logistics + bootprobe passed via `load` (when momentarily healthy). **‚öÝ ENV (still intermittent):** the standard `load` suite stalled on the THREE CDN this session ‚Äî the systems probes (officers/command/presets/‚Ä¶) were `load`-blocked, but the byte-identity harness exercises the full `fldSimStep`‚Üí`fldXFactorStep`‚Üí`fldOfficersStep` path (officers ON) for all 10 and proves it byte-identical, covering their core concern. **Re-run them next session once `load` is healthy** (serve via ThreadingHTTPServer; if `load` still stalls, the durable fix = domcontentloaded+settle in the probe runner OR vendor THREE locally ‚Äî a recommended small vetted milestone). **Bug-hunt** (23 Opus agents, 16 raw ‚Üí 4 confirmed + 3 critic, 0 HIGH, all LATENT@R-6): all 7 fixed (combined-speed clamp; cmdBonus surge gated to non-speed [one channel/badge]; apply decoupled from officers; vector bolt; grand_charge prov‚ÜíInferred + dual-downside deferred-note); catalog-wide badge-provenance sweep logged for R-6.

## ‚ö° CONTINUE HERE ‚Äî 2026-06-21 **CHICKAMAUGA ‚Äî the 3-phase Western epic shipped + adversarially hardened** (the woods ‚Üí Longstreet's breakthrough ‚Üí Thomas at Snodgrass Hill; probe 18/18) ‚Äî D90

A human US player who closes the Wood gap in P1 **overturns** the battle (the alt-history hinge). The CS won the field yet **bled MORE in aggregate** (~70k vs ~63k / 8 seeds) ‚Äî the costly-victory teaching, probe-guarded.

## ‚ö° CONTINUE HERE ‚Äî 2026-06-18 Custom Battle Builder C4 complete ‚úÖ ‚Äî single-phase authoring, import/export, slots, launch gate green

> **Custom Battle Builder C4 is built and verified.** New `src/tactical/T11-custom-battle.js` adds a first-class main-menu builder flow for player-authored real-time tactical scenarios. It covers scenario name/date/place, sides/briefs, objective, field size, terrain hills/woods/walls/markers, OOB units, artillery/gun counts, reinforcement/deployment timing, optional leaders, supply trains, teaching cards, provenance, JSON import/export, shareable JSON, and six local persistence slots.
>
> **Architecture decision:** C4 is intentionally **single-phase V1**. Phase authoring remains deferred until a UI for `phases[]` can be proven as safe as authored historical phase data. Custom scenarios do **not** enter `fldScenarioRegistry()`; `fldScenarioData(id)` only falls back to `fldCustomScenarioData(id)` for explicit `custom_...` IDs. That preserves the exact historical battle roster while still launching valid custom scenarios through the same single-phase `fldScenarioInit` data path. Field size is reset every launch via `FLD.BASE_FIELD_W/H`, then a scenario may apply `field.w/h` safely.
>
> **Validation guardrails:** required metadata, safe unique IDs, malformed/unsafe JSON keys, duplicate IDs, bounds and numeric clamps, objective placement, reinforcement timing, side ownership, leader attach ownership, realistic artillery crew counts (12-40 per gun), forbidden combat/damage keys, and `phases[]` are all blocked. Custom artillery uses the universal `guns` model only; no per-custom-battle damage fudge was added.
>
> **Focused probe:** `tools/probe-custom-battle-builder.mjs` verifies builder render, validation failures, valid scenario creation, export/import round trip, UI malformed-import rejection, slot save/list/load/delete, explicit custom-ID launch contract, universal gun model, field-size reset, no phase leak, no Classic `G.battle`, and no historical registry contamination. Current result: **9/9 steps ok, 0 fail**, with `tools/shots/probe-custom-battle-builder.json/png`.
>
> **Verification:** `node tools/build.mjs` ‚Üí GATE OK; `node tools/probe-custom-battle-builder.mjs` ‚Üí 9/9; `node tools/probe-tactical-roster.mjs` ‚Üí 8/8; `node tools/probe-field.mjs` ‚Üí 13/13; `node tools/probe-bullrun.mjs` ‚Üí 15/15; `node tools/probe-malvern-hill.mjs` ‚Üí 24/24; `node tools/probe-antietam.mjs` ‚Üí 16/16; `node tools/probe-fredericksburg.mjs` ‚Üí 22/22; `node tools/probe-chancellorsville.mjs` ‚Üí 24/24; `node tools/probe-gettysburg.mjs` ‚Üí 16/16; `node tools/probe-shiloh.mjs` ‚Üí 29/29; `node tools/probe-officers.mjs` ‚Üí 15/15; `node tools/probe-logistics.mjs` ‚Üí 14/14; `node tools/probe-arms.mjs` ‚Üí 23/23; `node tools/probe-presets.mjs` ‚Üí 26/26; `node tools/probe-csplayer.mjs` ‚Üí 16/16; `node tools/probe-campaign-link.mjs` ‚Üí 16/16; `node tools/probe-tactical-visuals.mjs` ‚Üí 6/6; `node tools/bootprobe.mjs` ‚Üí ok=true with known/tolerated 404 resource console entries; `node tools/t1probe.mjs` ‚Üí ok=true; `node tools/diag-classic.mjs` ‚Üí Classic paints, nonBlank 346; `git diff --check` ‚Üí clean.

## ‚ö° CONTINUE HERE ‚Äî run k (2026-06-16): **PHASE C-1.5 ¬∑ THE UNIVERSAL ARTILLERY GUN MODEL ‚úÖ SHIPPED + VETTED + PUSHED** ‚Üí IMMEDIATE NEXT = ANTIETAM as the MULTI-PHASE epic (D74 #1/#2)

> **The D74 "universal-combat" artillery cleanup ‚Äî the FIRST Antietam sub-milestone (do FIRST) ‚Äî is complete** (DECISIONS **D75**). Fredericksburg's per-battle **"volume-of-fire proxy men"** fudge (the C-1/D73 batteries inflated `men` to 500/440/500 to fake the massed crest fire) is REPLACED by a CONSISTENT gun-count model used identically in every battle. Deliverable ‚âà**1749.6KB**.
>
> **‚úÖ THE GUN MODEL (T5):** `FLDA.GUN_FIRE_WEIGHT` = 27 (men-equivalent fire-strength per gun, UNIVERSAL). `fldArtFireStr(u)` returns the fire-strength numerator (`fldResolveFire` divides by 1500): a battery with a GUN COUNT ‚Üí `guns * 27 * clamp(men/maxMen)` (rated fire from the gun count, crew-scaled so a battery fades smoothly as cannoneers fall); infantry / arms-off / a LEGACY no-`guns` battery ‚Üí `u.men` EXACTLY as before. `guns` carried data‚Üíunit via `fldMakeUnit` (T0) + `fldBrSpec` (T1); wired at `fldResolveFire`'s `strF`. CALIBRATED so a 6-gun battery ‚Üí 162 ‚âà Bull Run's realistic 160-men/6-gun Griffin & Ricketts ‚Üí the model REPRODUCES the existing batteries (consistent, not merely gated). The gun count is army-size-invariant "hardware" (strategic strength flows through the Cannon-Corps `_canisterScale`, not raw volume ‚Äî documented).
>
> **‚úÖ BYTE-IDENTITY:** the gun path is reached ONLY by a battery declaring `guns` (Fredericksburg's 3 crest batteries); every baseline has none ‚Üí `fldArtFireStr` returns `u.men` ‚Üí byte-identical. **field 13 ¬∑ bullrun 15 ¬∑ fog 13 ¬∑ autopause 13 ¬∑ ai 15 ¬∑ campaign-link 16 ¬∑ officers 15 ¬∑ logistics 14 ¬∑ presets 26 ¬∑ csplayer 16 ¬∑ arms 23** ‚Äî all byte-identical, 0 pe; bootprobe ok; t1probe 14; diag-classic **346**.
>

# HANDOFF ‚Äî "The Civil War" ‚Äî MASTER new-chat handoff (run h ‚Üí next build)

**Written 2026-06-13 (run h, Opus 4.8). THE single entry point for the next session.** Personal project ‚Äî NOT MJI. Full autonomy, Ultracode on, $0/free-CC0, build bar 200/100. **To start the next chat: paste the ¬ßPASTE block at the bottom.** Everything else here orients you.

## 1 ¬∑ THE PROJECT IN ONE PARAGRAPH
"The Civil War" is becoming **the definitive teaching wargame: Ultimate General: Gettysburg's combat FEEL + Paradox-grade strategic DEPTH + a museum's historical RIGOR** ‚Äî all three, no compromise. You are the **President (Lincoln or Davis)** running the entire war (economy, politics, diplomacy, morale, generals, the home front) AND commanding the battles in a real-time, gridless, drag-to-maneuver tactical engine ‚Äî wrapped in a PhD-level history + alternate-history teaching layer where scholarly consensus is the *favored-but-not-guaranteed* path. **The governing design law (Aaron's central tension, resolved): the simple low-micro UG:G battle is the always-fun CORE that stands alone; ALL depth is optional ‚Äî auto-managed by characterful advisors, delegable per-domain, preset-gated, fluidly dial-able; education is ambient, never blocks play, and confers real in-game mastery (so learning and fun pull the SAME direction).** One engine must serve the pure-battle player, the grand-strategist, and the PhD-historian simultaneously.

## 2 ¬∑ WHERE THINGS STAND (run h, verified)
- **Classic (hex, turn-based) is FROZEN/finished** ‚Äî the complete hex lineage + its 3D-skin "Modern." NEVER regress it (`tools/diag-classic.mjs` every splice).
- **Shipped + GPU-verified this run (all reusable):** procedural unit motion; **131 real PD-photo leader portraits** (`assets/portraits/`, license-gated, side-split for Anderson/Gregg) with a closure refactor + upgraded engraving fallback; a fuller period UI pass (drawn order-icons, engraved frames, brass portrait mat). Plus the inherited cinematic 3D foundation (PBR terrain, HDRI, ACES/bloom post-FX, weather, props, camera) and the adaptive period audio score.
- **The shipped "Modern" is only a 3D re-skin of the hex-turn engine** ‚Äî it does NOT play like UG:G. The real-time tactical engine + the grand-strategy owner-mode are **NOT built yet** ‚Äî that's the next work.
- **DESIGN: 63 decisions LOCKED** across a 35-round popup design session (Aaron). Fully captured in `GRAND-STRATEGY-PLAN.md` (Parts I‚ÄìIII). **No new-engine code written yet** ‚Äî the next chat builds from the spec.

## 3 ¬∑ THE DOCS (read in this order ‚Äî you have zero prior context)
1. **`GRAND-STRATEGY-PLAN.md`** ‚Äî THE DESIGN LAW. All 63 locked decisions: Part I (rounds 1‚Äì10: player/economy/executive/morale/alt-history/upgrades/education/victory/modes/first-build), Part II (rounds 11‚Äì20: diplomacy/slavery/politics/naval/map/generals/soldiers/intel/events/replay), Part III (rounds 21‚Äì33: **the depth‚Üîsimplicity balance** + presentation), ¬ß27 **the balance principle**, ¬ß13/¬ß24/¬ß28 decision indexes.

## 4 ¬∑ ARCHITECTURE DECISION (run h ‚Äî important)
**Modularize via a zero-dependency build step.** The scope (50‚Äì100k+ lines) outgrows the single 14k-line file. Author the new engine in **source modules**; a tiny **node concat script** assembles the one shippable `civil_war_generals.html` (keep the $0/portable/open-and-play deliverable + `play.command`). Set this up FIRST in S0. Classic + the existing engine stay intact through the transition (move them into the build later, carefully, or keep the current HTML as the base the build appends to). Gate the BUILT output (parse/hex/Classic-regression). This replaces the append-only-single-file splice model for new work ‚Äî but the gate discipline carries over.

## 5 ¬∑ BUILD ORDER & PHASES (Aaron: STRATEGIC-FIRST, confirmed twice)
**Phase group S (grand-strategy owner-mode) FIRST, then phase group P (real-time tactical).** Battles use the EXISTING engine via a clean bridge until the UG:G engine swaps in.
- **S0 ‚Äî scaffold:** set up the module/build system; expand the War Department (`G.campaign.{clock,muster,warroom}`) into the President's-desk shell (period war-room UI); strategic-turn loop; save. Layered scenario onboarding (start ~1861, limited toolset).
- **S1 ‚Äî economy** (full asymmetric model + finance/inflation/blockade).
- **S2 ‚Äî executive decisions + 3-layer morale + the 1864 election; the advisor/cabinet system** (the linchpin: auto-manage + recommend + TEACH, per-domain delegation).
- **S3 ‚Äî alt-history engine** (tiered divergence + hinge-points + emergent toggle + curated scenarios; deterministic-by-performance with consensus framing; the "your war vs history" tracker).
- **S4 ‚Äî education layer** (multi-voice debate cards + deep-dives + codex from HISTORICAL-DATA.md; ambient teaching; difficulty/realism sliders; play-style presets; full a11y).
- **S5 ‚Äî victory/defeat** (asymmetric paths incl. **negotiated peace for both sides**, military-only hard-loss) + all campaign scopes; wire existing battles through the bridge ‚Üí **playable full owner-mode war.**
- **THEN P0‚ÄìP5** (`MODERN-UGG-PLAN.md`): the real-time UG:G tactical engine (First Bull Run vertical slice first), swapping in behind the bridge.
Each phase: gate + real-GPU self-verify (probes you READ) + Classic no-regression + left in a working, polished state (ship-quality iteratively).

## 6 ¬∑ THE BALANCE PRINCIPLE (design law ‚Äî apply to EVERY system)
The simple, low-micro UG:G battle is the always-fun core that works on its own. Every deep system is optional ‚Äî auto-managed by characterful advisors, delegable per-domain, preset-gated, fluidly dial-able mid-campaign. Education is ambient, never blocks play, and confers real mastery (learning is rewarded by winning, not a chore-score). Presets + sliders let each player set their own balance. **If a feature forces depth on a battle-first player, it's wrong; if it denies depth to a strategist/historian, it's wrong.** (Full statement: GRAND-STRATEGY-PLAN ¬ß27.)

## 7 ¬∑ TOOLCHAIN, GATES, GOTCHAS (proven ‚Äî reuse)
- **Gates every change:** `.bak` ‚Üí parse (`node --check` the built/extracted `<script>`) ‚Üí invalid-hex grep `0x[0-9a-fA-F]*[g-z]` = 0 ‚Üí collision-grep new fns = 0. With the new build step, gate the assembled output.
- **Real-GPU self-verify (READ the PNGs/probes):** `tools/shot-postfx.mjs`, `tools/shot-gpu.mjs`, `tools/shot-ui.mjs`, `tools/probe-motion.mjs`, `tools/probe-portraits.mjs`, `tools/bootprobe.mjs`, `tools/diag-classic.mjs`. Real GPU = **Intel UHD 617** via headed Chrome `--use-angle=metal`. A real-time sim/strategic loop needs an EMPIRICAL probe (sample state over frames), not just screenshots. Stale server: `lsof -ti tcp:8765 | xargs kill`.
- **Perf target:** smooth on the Intel UHD 617 at Auto tier; instancing/LOD/perf-tiers mandatory.
- **CRITICAL gotchas:** `G`/`HEX`/`PALETTE`/`THREE_BASE` are bare-name lexical globals (never `window.G`); THREE loads async (no top-level `new THREE.*`); override-by-redeclaration (last def wins); never a literal `*/` in a block comment; honor `reduceMotion` + `gfxQuality`; **NEVER regress Classic**; $0/free-CC0; Verified/Inferred provenance on all history.
- **Asset pipeline (historical run-H note; current top block supersedes live setup):** PD images via the run-h portrait pattern (Wikipedia REST summary ‚Üí Commons license API PD-gate ‚Üí download ‚Üí `sips` resize). Extend to weapons/flags/USCT. Blender MCP remains available for future explicit 3D asset jobs (PolyHaven CC0 / Sketchfab), but Blender does not need to stay open unless a Phase-H asset task starts; free Hyper3D trial is drained.
